Procedures and Escort Issues for Exhibits Participating in the British Arts Exhibition

The Preparatory Committee Has Decided on Proper Measures

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 29th) The Preparatory Committee for the British Exhibition of Chinese Art has decided on the procedures for exhibiting items and protecting and transporting them as follows: (A) Before the items leave the country (1) The preliminary list of exhibits will be drawn up by the special committee of the Chinese Preparatory Committee and the producing agency, but the Preparatory Committee reserves the right to retain items it deems particularly important. (2) Items intended for exhibition that belong to the Palace Museum and the Antiquities Exhibition Hall will be submitted by the museum, still stored in the original warehouse, and items solicited from other public and private institutions will be directly handed over to the Custody Committee for storage in the bank vault. They may not be withdrawn without the stamp of the Preparatory Committee and the Custody Committee on the withdrawal list. (3) In February, a second selection meeting will be held at the Bank of China building on the Bund in Shanghai, and the Chinese special committee will review the items for export. The British selection committee may make suggestions, but the Preparatory Committee has the final decision-making power. (4) Items intended for exhibition must be pre-exhibited domestically and are scheduled to be held in March at the former site of the Bank of China on the Bund in Shanghai. (5) Before the items leave the country, a detailed catalog must be printed and attached with photographs to show credibility. (6) All exported items must be stamped or affixed with a seal or other appropriate mark, and the seal pattern must be submitted to the Preparatory Committee for verification after returning to China. (7) During the pre-exhibition, the antiquities of the Palace Museum and the Antiquities Exhibition Hall will be handled by the responsible personnel designated by the museum together with the Preparatory Committee. (8) During the pre-exhibition period, the Preparatory Committee and the Palace Museum will send personnel to work day and night. There must be security guards stationed in the venue. (9) During the pre-exhibition, there must be sufficient police and plainclothes detectives to protect the venue, and patrol police must be added day and night. (10) After the pre-exhibition, Chinese and British personnel will supervise the packaging, experts will pack the boxes, and porcelain and copper utensils will first be packed in small boxes, with the items marked outside the box, and then packed in large boxes with the contents clearly marked, and the items will be packed tightly so that they cannot be moved. Other items should also be properly packaged, and then sealed and stamped jointly by Chinese and British committee members. (11) After the items are packed, if they need to wait for the ship to depart, the items from the Palace Museum and the Antiquities Exhibition Hall will still be sent to the original warehouse for storage, and other public and private items solicited will be stored by the Custody Committee.

(B) When the Items Leave the Country (12) When the items are loaded onto the ship, they must be escorted by security guards. (13) The items must be stored in a proper place after being loaded onto the ship and must not be moved along the way. (14) The ship transporting the items will be taken care of and protected by Chinese representatives and guards. (15) When the items leave the country, they will be escorted by British warships from Shanghai to Singapore, and on the return journey, they will be escorted from Singapore to Shanghai.

(C) After the Items Arrive in the UK (16) After the ship arrives in London and enters the port, the representatives of the Royal Academy of Arts and the police will pick them up and transport them to the Royal Academy of Arts. After the Chinese representatives check the number of boxes, the items will be stored in the storage of the Royal Academy, sealed off, and guarded day and night by capable police. (17) British customs will not inspect the items at the dock. If the boxes need to be opened, they must be opened at the Royal Academy of Arts under the supervision of the Chinese representatives. (18) The Executive Committee jointly formed by China and Britain is responsible for all matters related to the exhibition of items in the UK. (19) During the exhibition period, a sufficient number of police and plainclothes detectives will protect the exhibits during the day. All doors will be locked at night. In addition to the regular police, patrol police will be added. (20) Security guards will be stationed at the exhibition venue to provide special protection. (21) Items must be locked in display cabinets during the exhibition.

(D) When the Items Return to China and After They Return (22) The public and private items exhibited by China this time are exclusively for the London exhibition and may not be sold, exchanged, or donated, nor may they be exhibited elsewhere. (23) The same protection measures will be taken when the items are shipped back to China as when they were shipped abroad. (24) After the items return to China, the Preparatory Committee will conduct a detailed inspection and hold an exhibition in Nanjing once. (25) The antiquities of the Palace Museum and the Antiquities Exhibition Hall will be inspected and recovered by the museum. The items solicited from other public and private institutions will be returned by the Custody Committee. (26) After the event, all the circumstances of the exhibition will be reported to the Executive Yuan by the Preparatory Committee and forwarded to the Central Government, and a special book will be published.

All Primary Schools in Jiangsu Province Are Organized into Baojia

Cultivating Students' Self-Government Ability

Zhenjiang News: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs previously reported that the Jiangpu County Government requested that all primary schools at all levels in the county be organized into Baojia in order to cultivate students' self-government ability and instill Baojia common sense. After review, the proposed measures were deemed feasible, so a special request was made to the Department of Education to order all other counties to follow suit. According to inquiries, the main points of the Baojia organization measures in Jiangpu County schools are as follows: When organizing, the entire school is regarded as a township, one classroom as one Bao, a horizontal row as one Jia, and each student as one household. Single-grade primary schools only have one Bao. Schools with six or more classrooms can be organized into two townships. Two or more townships can form a district. The district has one district chief, who is elected by the district people's congress. When starting the organization, doorplates are affixed to each student's desk. After the organization is clear, each Jia will jointly issue a joint guarantee, add fingerprints, and declare mutual supervision and compliance with school rules. In addition, Baojia regulations are formulated to implement the new life as the goal. When students graduate, drop out, take leave of absence, and enroll, they should fill out the household registration change form in accordance with the regulations and report it to the principal at each level.

Ministry of Education Explains the Method for Retroactively Recognizing the Qualifications of Graduates Before Establishment

Because China College requested an explanation of the method for retroactively recognizing the qualifications of graduates before establishment, the Ministry of Education specially instructed the school to still follow Article 6 of Instruction No. 8699 of the 22nd year. (Check the clause, which says that graduates who fail to obtain retroactive recognition according to the previous standards may request the original school to submit to the Ministry a request to take the qualification examination for graduates of private junior colleges or above before establishment. The method is as follows: (A) In accordance with the conditions for requesting retroactive recognition specified in Article 5, the original school shall submit the application to the Ministry for approval and registration. (B) The qualification examination shall be held regularly by the Ministry. One month before the examination, the Ministry shall publish a notice in the newspaper to inform the students who have been approved for registration. (C) The examination subjects are divided into two categories: general and specialized. The general subjects are Chinese and Party Ideology (the Three Principles of the People). There are five to eight specialized subjects, and they will also be notified one month before the examination. (D) Graduates who pass the qualification examination will have their graduation qualifications recognized. (E) Each student may take the qualification examination for a maximum of two times.

Sports News

Furen Lost to McLing

Evenly Matched, Fierce Competition

McLing's Locke Scored 30 Points Alone

Result: 44 to 37

Tonight, Furen Faces West Blue

The Beijing Furen University basketball team fought hard last night but still lost to McLing, with a score of 37 to 44. The Shenyuan basketball hall was filled with 800 to 900 spectators, creating a grand atmosphere. The overall situation was tense and exciting, with intense interest. After Furen initially took the lead, they followed McLing except for three leads at 7-5, 17-15, and 19-17. The first half saw several ties at 7-7, 15-15, 17-17, and 19-19, eventually losing the first half 19-23. In the second half, they made great efforts, showing a potential to come from behind, but ultimately failed to achieve their goals. In the end, they lost opportunities due to panic and were defeated.

Locke Rampant

The Shenyuan court was too large, leading to a sense of exhaustion. Furen moved quickly, but sometimes acted too hastily, missing opportunities. Forwards Li Yunzhong and Liu Xueqi were active and capable, deserving praise as outstanding talents. Guard Zhao Lin's defense was tight and indispensable. The entire team worked closely together, but lost many opportunities under the basket in the last five minutes, leading to their defeat, which was a pity. Moreover, they suffered from being shorter. McLing's long-legged Locke acted rampantly, scoring as many as 30 points alone. McLing's victory was entirely due to this man.

Overwhelming Momentum

After the initial contact, Furen's Li Yunzhong scored first, leading to 3-3 and then 5-5. After a brief stalemate, Liu Xueqi scored again under the basket, leading 7-5. McLing was like wolves and tigers, with overwhelming momentum. Locke and Billis scored five consecutive points, taking the lead at 10-7. At the same time, Furen's guard Lian Cheng was fouled out for the fourth time and replaced by Li Yunwu. Then, Locke and Johnson added three more points, taking a commanding lead at 13-7.

Furen Strives

Furen was eager to win, unwilling to fall behind, striving and showing a new spirit. Liu Xueqi and Zhao Lin caught up with three points. After McLing's Locke scored again, making it 15-10, Liu added three more points, and Li Yunwu made two consecutive free throws, tying the score at 15-15. The atmosphere in the whole stadium was tense, and the shouts were deafening. Li Yunzhong then scored again, achieving a 17-15 lead, and before the cheers subsided, McLing's Johnson returned the favor, immediately tying the score at 17. Li Yunzhong scored again, leading 19-17. Locke made two free throws, tying the score again. In an instant, Locke added two more goals, and McLing won the first half 23-19.

Running out of steam

At the restart, Locke of McLing stood out from the crowd, taking advantage and scoring repeatedly. Furen's guards found it difficult to defend. Wu Bixian and Li Yunzhong also contributed, but their gains did not make up for their losses, and the score once became 33-24, a difference of as many as nine points. At this time, Furen was truly facing a difficult situation. Their formation was chaotic, Li Yunwu was short and suffered losses, and Zhao Lin was unable to attend to everything, unable to respond in time.

Panic and Missed Opportunities

Furen tried their best to cheer up and slowly expand their plan. After Liu Xueqi and Wu Bixian added two goals in a row, their momentum suddenly surged, and they continued to work harder and became more energetic. Liu Xueqi scored repeatedly with close-range shots and long-range shots, chasing the score to 32-34, only two points behind, showing a great potential to come from behind. McLing's formation was disorganized, and Locke was heavily guarded and unable to do anything. After 36-38, Furen suddenly became eager to win, missed opportunities under the basket, and were extremely flustered. Then, with a moment of carelessness in the back, Locke showed his power again, and the score soared to 44-37, marking Furen's defeat.

Playing Against West Blue

Tonight is Furen's last battle in Shanghai, against West Blue, the basketball champion. Since the beginning of the season, this team has never been defeated. Furen's chances against them are slim, but if they can be cautious and fight calmly, they may be able to win by surprise. The game will still be held at Shenyuan at 8:30 tonight. Free Talk

On the Monk Not Running Away

— Zai Qing

Liu Bannong, one of the most active figures in the early New Literature Movement, passed away in 1934. He left behind many works, especially the posthumously published "Bannong Essays," which is an important document in the history of the Chinese New Literature Movement. At the beginning of this book, he wrote a long preface explaining his attitude towards writing, his experiences, and the motivation for compiling the collection. At the end, he wrote a popular folk story in his usual humorous manner.

It is said that a constable was assigned to escort a monk. He was carrying a document, a bag of clothes, an umbrella, and a cangue on the monk's head. Along the way, the constable was afraid of losing anything, so he kept chanting: "Monk, document, clothes bag, umbrella, cangue." One night, the monk took advantage of the constable's deep sleep, shaved the constable's head, put his own cangue on the constable's neck, and secretly escaped. When the constable woke up, he touched his head and checked the things. The monk was there, the document was there, the clothes bag was there, the umbrella was there, only he himself was not there, "I don't know where I went."

After telling this story, he wrote below: "The so-called grasping the spirit of the times, the so-called standing in front of the times, I have never stopped envying and longing for this kind of beautiful talk. However, I am unwilling to grasp the monk and lose myself." The meaning is very clear, that is, literature that stands in front of the times and grasps the spirit of the times essentially lacks the existence of "self." Grasping the times and losing myself is like the monk running away and the constable being caught. He is unwilling to do this.

"Did the monk really run away?" I thought so when I read this passage. Before writing this article, I read Zhang Menglin's article on the settlement of Chinese literature in 1934 in "New China." In the part on essays, his conclusion is that essays are only personal subjective literature. This is indeed the case. The pity is that he did not know that in the essays of 1934, there was also a tendency to oppose the individual and oppose subjectivity. Liu Bannong knew that there was a "monk" besides the "constable," which can be said to be a step higher than Zhang Menglin. But in the end, he was dazzled. If he had not died and had rubbed his eyes, he would have definitely seen that the "constable" was still there, and the "monk" had not run away. The one who created this environment was his own dim eyes.

He thinks so, and maybe more others think so. Literature that is anti-individualistic and anti-subjective fundamentally has no "individual" and has lost the existence of "self." Actually, it is not so. It is said that there was such a thing. A temporary actor participated in the filming of a crowd scene. When the film was released, he proudly ran to the theater to watch it. Sure enough, the crowd scene he participated in the filming also appeared. There were so many people on one screen that he could not count them. However, he was sad. He could not see his own existence. He was annoyed by his own sacrifice. He almost cried. But in a flash, the screen faded into a part of the crowd. He saw his whole body, "So there is me." He was a little happy. Because he was next to the protagonist, the screen faded in again. He felt that he was too clear. He looked at the protagonist's big head: "So there are so many Jiang

people in him." He was no longer sad. The one who told the story of "the constable and the monk" essentially only saw the first screen in the movie during his lifetime.

What I am saying here may not fully express his original intention. The "monk" he was talking about may refer to the "consistency in thoughts and propositions" that I am talking about. This consistency is "someone else's" and not "one's own." Let's go back to his golden age in literature. He wrote "A Reply to Mr. Wang Jingxuan's Letter." He opposed the remnants of old literature. He advocated vernacular literature. But the promotion of vernacular literature did not begin with Liu Bannong. Then, in the early days of the New Literature Movement, wasn't he also a person who "grasped the monk and lost himself"? We cannot say that. There was still his own existence in it. This existing self was still very clear, and he himself probably would admit it.

Now it is different from the May Fourth period, and the "self" reflected in literature has changed. This change made him sigh, "Why don't I want to?" What has changed? It is that the "self" at that time was only dissolved in the lives of a few people, and the life of "self" only had consistency with a few people, so the existence of "self" was particularly obvious. Now, the times have progressed. People who grasp the spirit of the times are expanding the "self" and dissolving the life of "self" in the lives of most people. In the eyes of Liu Bannong and his group, the "self" is blurred, even submerged. In fact, what is grasped is "the monk" and also "the self."

It can be further explained. The current "self" is like the first screen mentioned above. The self exists, but because it is dissolved with everyone, it is not easy to see. The past self, such as the second and even the third independent screen, only dissolved a few people, and it was clear at a glance. It is easy to recognize people in strange clothes among the crowd, but it is not easy to find people in ordinary clothes. The reason is the same. The question is, does "self" want to be dissolved among a few people or among most people? Be careful that "the monk" runs away.

Self-Comfort

— Wei Zhongtian

The past life was like mud and stagnant water, but I prefer to relive those lives that resemble mud and stagnant water. Today, in today's memories, half of my heart is in pain, and the other half feels slightly comforted. In recent years, my life has been too complicated, with blood, terror, and tears, but also laughter. I don't know how many times in my dreams, I dreamed of those terrible encounters in the past, making me scream and fear until I woke up and realized it was just a nightmare!

However, in the mud, my heart can still bloom with pure white flowers. I can comfort myself with this.

Friends, think about it, how can people not be thin under the double squeeze of poverty and hunger? How can people not grow old! One by one, the enemy's hidden arrows were shot at my heart. I was injured. People would die if they were a little weaker. Fortunately, I am still alive and strong. In the past, there were several nights when I really wanted to leave this world quietly. However, this was just "thinking." In fact, I am still alive in this world. This world is evil and filthy, but how many people are hiding in the filth, laughing and singing triumphantly, feeling happy! I really don't understand why people's hearts are so far apart.

This time last year, my heart was being bitten by thousands of snakes, making me unable to shout or cry! This year, at this time, it seems to be a little better on the outside, but I am still enduring hidden pain to live my life.

Zhen came to play last night. He is also a person who has experienced many terrible events like me. His face is always sad and melancholy. Although I also have his share of sadness and melancholy in my heart, I still deliberately weave a lot of sweet words to comfort him and tell him not to be discouraged, but he doesn't like to listen because he knows the world better than I do. Sometimes I seem to feel that it is better for a person to have no wisdom or knowledge. Knowledge, knowledge can become a poisonous substance in some people's minds, so some people are willing to be buried in the graves they have dug themselves. Do you say he took the wrong path? No, in fact, he才said that you took the wrong path. What can be done?

The sea, the desert, agriculture and forestry, the city, the battlefield, hell, ······ I have traveled all over, making me accustomed to all kinds of hardships. The storms of the night, the darkness of hell, the iron whip of life, and the poisonous hidden arrows, I have all tasted. So, perhaps there will be an even heavier burden of suffering on my shoulders in the future, but I am not afraid because I am used to it.

I have seen many people subdued under the iron whip of life, but I am still willing to struggle in a harsh environment. Although it is苦, I also feel that it is worth it because this is what I am willing to do. Is there anything in the world more precious than freedom? No! Therefore, although the past life is like mud and stagnant water, my heart is blooming with pure white flowers in the mud. This is worth self-comfort!

The Hunter (Part 2)

— Shi Dai

Usually, it felt like just a moment to reach the Gurbantunggut Mountains, but today it seems the further I go, the further it gets. I've been walking for ages and still can't see a shadow of the Gurbantunggut Mountains. What's wrong? It must be that the horse is running too slow! Torgut Nalhar was furious! He reached for the whip on his belt, but it was empty. He was in too much of a hurry and forgot to bring the whip, which brought a little regret. This made him even angrier! He twisted his body and punched the horse's rump hard with his fist:

Damn it! You're deliberately messing with me!

The horse threw its hooves wide and galloped swiftly as if taking flight. Its pure white, spotless short hair was soaked with sweat, and it exhaled hot air from its mouth, panting and using all its strength.

Bang!

Suddenly, a gunshot rang out, and Torgut Nalhar's eyes followed the sound. In the distance, a group of people were coming from the north of Bogda Feng, all on horseback. Torgut Nalhar stopped his horse and looked carefully. They were all carrying weapons, like a band of bandits, running towards him. Torgut Nalhar felt uneasy. If bandits really caught him, there would be no chance of survival.

The best of the thirty-six tactics is to flee! He made up his mind and spurred his horse to run. Gunshots continued to ring out behind him.

Thud!

The horse stumbled and fell. This was more dangerous than a bullet entering Torgut Nalhar's chest! Torgut Nalhar dismounted and stood still, facing the approaching horsemen, arms outstretched, standing as if he had lost consciousness, waiting for the judgment of fate.

Coldness sprayed from the snowy ground, encroaching on the Alag Mountain plain. Every cell in Torgut Nalhar's body was being toyed with by the cold. The pure white horse lay on the snow, and it was almost impossible to tell what was horse and what was snow. The horse's panting mingled with Torgut Nalhar's faint breathing, and the sun stared intently at Torgut Nalhar's furrowed brow.

Torgut Nalhar hung his head, his eyes blurred, as if he had been sculpted by the cold onto the snow.

× × ×

When Torgut Nalhar looked up, the fear instantly shattered and disappeared in his heart! It turned out that these people were all soldiers of the Bayin King's bandit suppression army.

Before he could speak, someone grabbed him:

See where you can escape now!

The color immediately drained from Torgut Nalhar's face, and he stared wide-eyed in terror:

You've mistaken me for someone else. I'm a hunter from Kamu Luto!

Another man with a beard approached Torgut Nalhar and shouted:

Bastard! You stole Lama Laiyin's livestock and won't admit it! We'll see if you confess today. You don't need anything else; the horse you're riding is Lama Laiyin's!

Torgut Nalhar looked up at the sky, tears streaming down his face, and said nothing, knowing that arguing would be a waste of words.

Three or four young men tied Torgut Nalhar's back, and two men with sabers dragged him away.

The sky was clear, the ground was snow-white, and the horse was pure white and spotless. Only humanity was impure. Sabers, purple robes, yellow jackets, horses of all colors, and Torgut Nalhar's heart!

On the vast, boundless plain, the white, crystalline snow covered all the dust and dirt. Horseshoes left tracks in the snow, and the cold branded people's faces. In this empty plain, silence drove away the wind and all sounds. At this moment, only the sound of hooves and panting, sabers and daggers, broke through the defenses of silence, using commotion to resist the cold.

Victory appeared on the face of every soldier, the dark purple faces radiating the greatness of the Khalkha people! Torgut Nalhar was no longer a hunter at all; he had simply disgraced the hunters! How could he have lost his resistance, with no trace of the Khalkha spirit!

The horseshoes disappeared under the snow, and the men dismounted, surrounding Torgut Nalhar to see Lama Laiyin.

But someone had already been sent there to deliver a message:

The Living Buddha has instructed that the horse thief be caught and killed without being brought to him.

Torgut Nalhar couldn't even squeeze out any tears. Others had already announced his crimes, and then they would carry out the death penalty.

Living Buddha, take me to heaven!

Torgut Nalhar knelt straight and still, praying, closing his eyes and waiting for the final outcome.

Suddenly, a storm rose, and the snow on the ground was swept up, rustling. The snow on the yurt was blown to the ground by the wind, the horses neighed, the Khalkha people's blood boiled, and in a burst of shouts, Torgut Nalhar's blood splattered on the snow.

Lama Laiyin knelt before the Buddha and prayed:

May my Buddha bless Torgut Nalhar to ascend to heaven; his sins have been atoned for.

The wind howled, the snow flew, and the Mongolian plain was immersed in cold. (The End)

Eating (2)

— Zhou Wen

"Hey, tell me, why is this rice always so bad?"

I saw him staring greedily at my cigarette, which really surprised me. While guarding it, I casually said:

"Who knows? I'm hungry, just eat it, why ask?"

"No, I mean, this rice is from..."

I saw that he hadn't finished speaking, and he moved a step closer to me. His starving look made me have to be even more cautious. I held the cigarette butt in my palm with my fingers and replied casually:

"Don't worry about it..."

"Look!" Helplessly, he pointed a finger at a classmate on the horizontal bar, doing cartwheels. "Ha, another one!" He simply shouted at him. Immediately, the classmates watching around the horizontal bar, with their mouths open, laughed and echoed:

"Good, another one!"

The classmate with the rough face on the iron bar was flashing a pair of burning eyes. I saw that he was actually very hungry. However, in the cheers of the crowd, a surge of heroic spirit suddenly adorned his brow. His face flushed, and his blue veins bulged. He said "ha" and I was worried that he would pour out all his breastfeeding strength. But he already had his feet towards the sky and his bald head towards the ground. In the blink of an eye, he had flipped a round somersault around the round iron bar. Everyone seemed to be watching with interest, and some seemed to feel that this hungry fool should just turn out even his breastfeeding strength, so they slipped out and shouted:

"Good, another one!"

Then another round somersault. By the time of the third "another one", the cigarette butt in my palm suddenly left my fingers. Turning around, I saw that the classmate next to me had already stuffed the cigarette butt in his mouth and jumped into the crowd.

On Poetry and Emotion

— Liu Bing

Some poets have said: "Express your emotions completely; that is where poetry lies." Although we cannot fully agree with this statement, "art - poetry is the use of concrete images to express thoughts and feelings," especially poetry that expresses the highest emotions, its inseparable connection with emotion is very obvious.

Recently, some poets have written poems like this - poems without emotion. We all know that art is one of the means of spiritual connection between people. The higher the emotion expressed in a work of art, the more it can arouse the possibility of spiritual connection. Conversely, if the art given cannot convey the author's spirit to the reader, the work loses its value. A poem without emotion is like a skeleton without marrow, a news report in rhyming lines.

However, we must also note that in the society we live in, the things we see, the things we hear, and all kinds of facts can stir our emotions. Do all these emotions have the value of being expressed in poetry? We can say affirmatively, no!

Regarding this point, Ruskin once said: "A maiden can sing about lost love, but a miser cannot sing about lost money." He also said: "Regarding the emotion that grips you tightly, this emotion is sung by the poet, actively and in the true sense. Ask yourself if it can move him? If it can, this emotion is good; if it cannot be sung, then only the ridiculous aspect gives emotion, and that emotion is low."

Here, it clearly tells us the reason why not all emotions have the value of being expressed in poetry. For example, a miser losing money also has his own inner emotional flow. Why can't he sing about it? Clearly, it is because it is useless for connection between people.

How do we determine which emotions are worth expressing? This is not only determined by the degree of burning excitement of the poet, but also by the needs of real society. Not long after the May Fourth Movement, romantic songs of love were favored by people, but after the May 30th Movement, they were despised by those who loved them. At that time, violent, passionate, and shouting emotions were sung by people.

At the same time, this includes the poet's artistic view - worldview. For example, the emotions of a leisured poet about singing about unrequited love will inevitably be spat upon by the working masses. Conversely, singing about positive emotions will inevitably be despised by the leisured.

Finally, I will use the words of Mori Yama Kei as the conclusion of this article:

"First, the thing that has value in being expressed in poetry is always the need of a certain society. All poets base that need on the poet's worldview and the crucible of emotion, and express it in poetry. Second, therefore, the more the poet's crucible of emotion can boil for the task of realizing the historical progress of society, the more the value of that emotion will be increased when expressed in poetry."

Customs Gold Plummets, Gold Market Weakens Initially But Then Firms Up, Forward Discount Recovers Slightly

The gold market was initially weak but then firmed up yesterday, resulting in a stable outcome. There were no special stimuli throughout the day. Securities

January Public Bonds Hampered by the Environment

Yesterday, January 29th, was the settlement date for the January futures contracts at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange. The total settlement amount was 41,140,000 yuan. Among this, brokers settled 22,770,000 yuan through mutual account transfers, while 18,370,000 yuan was settled at the exchange. This amount is not insignificant, and the off-exchange settlement amount is not included. This shows that although credit is tight, the public's faith in government bonds remains strong. The majority of sellers were from the financial sector, while the buyers were mostly small groups and individual investors. Since the market downturn, various enterprises have become unviable, and the closure of large and small businesses and small banks has been frequently reported. Therefore, idle funds have actually increased, and most investors have concentrated on government bonds, seeking their stable returns. If the environment can be somewhat stabilized, bond prices may still tend to rise. The January futures market opened on November 29th of last year. The initial market prices were 73.5 yuan for Disbandment Bonds and 55.5 yuan for Salt Tax Bonds. At that time, due to the increasingly close cooperation between the Southwest factions and the unquestioned passage of the Fifth Plenary Session, the market price on December 3rd rose to 76.5 yuan for Disbandment Bonds and 57.8 yuan for Salt Tax Bonds. Subsequently, due to the gradual tightening of credit, the daily increase in foreign exchange rates, and the resignation of Huang Fu, etc., the financial sector sold off daily, and arbitrage trading did not occur. On December 17th, there was another slight decline, with Disbandment Bonds falling to 72.85 yuan and Salt Tax Bonds to 53.8 yuan, a difference of about 4 yuan. This high and low fluctuation lasted only two weeks. Afterwards, foreign exchange rates declined from high levels, the Flat Market Committee transported silver back to Shanghai from Hong Kong, and the postal communication problem was resolved. The market price gradually returned to normal. In between, rumors of currency devaluation and inflation caused a period of market turmoil, with erratic fluctuations. Recently, the issue of the Chahar conflict has caused significant changes in market prices, but they have risen and fallen accordingly without much impact. Considering that the financial sector sold a lot, but buyers were still very active, the total transaction volume for one month was 38,022,500 yuan. According to the report from New China Trading Company, yesterday (28th), the New York stock market was sluggish and lifeless. Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Remarks by the President of an American University

— Wan

Houston, USA, 25th. Dr. Wei Zhuoming, President of West China Union University, today declared that China cannot continue to allow itself to be slaughtered by Japan's aggressive actions. It should rely on its own strength to resist, and so on.

I do not know what the purpose of the president's advocacy of such remarks is. Is it merely to encourage China to resist Japan? If that is the case, then the president's words are rather ridiculous. Japan's aggression against China is not only a matter for China and Japan; it is a matter that concerns all countries in the world, but with varying degrees of severity. The heavy losses suffered by us from Japan's direct slaughter are self-evident, but do other countries not have any relation to this matter? But the president said, "Our country (referring to the United States) can accept Japan's policy in pursuit of peace, but China should rely on its own strength to resist." This view of the Sino-Japanese problem as a local issue in the Far East, unrelated to countries around the world, is in line with the American's long-held Monroe Doctrine: "Everyone sweeps the snow from his own doorstep and does not care about the frost on others' roofs."

But the president also said, "Japan's aggression against China is obviously a preliminary step to drive the white race out of Asia." If so, then the president recognizes that Japan's encroachment on China is not just a local problem in the Far East, but has a global presence. But the president also said that the United States Navy is not protecting the Philippines and Hawaii, and that it would be easy for Japan to seize these two places, thus indicating that the United States cannot help and can stay out of the matter, already revealing the intention that other countries should come forward to intervene.

The president also said, "Japan's recent ambition is to find a market for selling Japanese goods. China advocates open doors, while Japan advocates the Monroe Doctrine in Asia." Advocating open doors means that China is a market for many countries; advocating the Monroe Doctrine means that China is a market for Japan alone. It does not matter whether China is someone else's market. Regardless, it is an undeniable fact that China's national power is still unable to resist the Japanese at this time. Even if it were possible, on the one hand, we would be resisting for the sake of our own country, and on the other hand, we would be resisting for the sake of the great powers, which would bring little benefit to our own country.

In short, the world today is truly as the ancients said, "Move one hair, and the whole body is affected." The situation in Europe is no different from that in the Far East. Germany's abandonment of alliances, regardless of everything, and its desperate hard work are no different from Japan. However, France's national strength is far more substantial than that of China, but France is unable to contain its powerful neighbors' tyranny. It must rely on the strength of Britain and Italy, as well as the smaller countries, to control Germany's power. Thus, any country that wants to resist a tyrannical neighbor must rely on allied countries. It cannot be accomplished by a single country, as can be seen in this example.

Elegy

— Qi Wu

It seemed I was discovered only when I reached the third hall.

The situation in the hall was different. Did you think it would be even more desolate here? Quite the opposite! Like a large gathering, all the members of the clan were present. Although a row of white mourning colors made people feel uncomfortable, as if a stone were hanging from their hearts, it was noisy here. This restless atmosphere seemed somewhat inconsistent with the fact that my father had passed away.

Because I was eager to see my aunt, the maid told me she was in the bedroom, so I went upstairs.

My aunt was sleeping on the bed with her clothes on, sound asleep. Was this widow's grief, in her dreams, unaware that all the housework had not been properly arranged by her uncle?

When I came downstairs again, I saw the noisy heads clearly. Since my grandfather's death, I had never seen such "liveliness." Many familiar faces had increased by at least one-third. In their noisy state, my sudden appearance did not attract their attention, but my mother and younger brother called out to me from a dark corner. Before I could open my mouth, my mother quietly warned me with her eyes:

"Listen!"

Indeed, I had stepped into unfamiliar territory. Everyone, every face, every action, every word, seemed to be cut off from me, and my mother was saying that to me. Rather than speculating, I sat down in a chair in the corner, like an audience waiting for the curtain to rise.

A jumble of words reached my ears, but you couldn't tell who was speaking, except for a rough voice that shouted, "What's all the noise about? Speak properly!" Hearing his words, you could tell that the person was so forthright, like a swarm of flies chasing after something rotten. There was no intention to insult here, but do you know what they were arguing about? The inheritance, which was as welcome to the swarm of flies as something rotten!

I understood this "lively" situation. I lowered my head and retreated to the second hall. My uncle's appearance alone in the center was so terrible that it made me wonder if there really was a soul after death. He had been diligent and thrifty all his life, but the cost of his medical treatment was so great that he couldn't even enjoy

Page 18

the pleasure of listening to the radio. He was worn out by "housework" and died. I can say that with certainty.

I said earlier that this mansion was maintained by my uncle, this weak pillar, bearing the entire weight. Usually, no one would step forward to say a word about even the smallest trivial matters, and that one word could determine whether or not the "matter" was settled. As an uncle, he did not fall ill from being too diligent in housework, but what was it that pulled him back to his hometown when he wanted to listen to the radio? He was the master of this mansion, and he could not waste the ancestral inheritance too much. He had to set a good example for others. We don't ask whether spending money on medical treatment was wasting the ancestral property, but that was not the biggest reason. He was disregarding his own weak strength and wanted to support the permanent existence of this mansion. He could not sit idly by and watch no one stand up for this large clan!

But this mansion was eventually collapsing. Unexpectedly, there were so many ultra-"lively" people who would take charge of the overall situation because my uncle did not have a son!

I cautiously raised my head and surveyed those familiar faces. I wanted to cry, but there were no tears! (The End)

Longing and Terror

— Xue Hong

Time has taken away twenty-one years from me without any hesitation. I once floated through these past journeys, as if I were sitting on a train passing through a distant road in a short period of time. With my eyes open, I looked at the lush branches along the road, as well as the vast, verdant, and fertile fields in the distance, and my heart was always filled with light laughter! My face was also always filled with a pleasant color. In the past journey, I also seemed to be riding an airplane soaring in the boundless sky. Although it was only for a moment, I did feel the joy of traveling: the light, sparkling, and beautiful clouds floated into the cabin window, making me confused and intoxicated; in the blue, clear sky and the vast, distant world, I looked up and down, feeling that I had reached a state of "forgetting myself" and "I am nothing"! The human world seemed to have nothing to do with me.

If it were possible, I would shout to the driver to slam on the train's engine; or I would prohibit the pilot of the plane from stopping the flight. Because at this time, I had taken all the scenery into my eyes and marveled at it, and I really didn't want to move forward to hurt my good eyesight!

If it were possible, I also wished the train or plane would hurry back and review my past journey again. Because I knew that my progress did not have any predetermined goals, my initial intention was just to play and just to try! Now I have had enough of this game and this attempt, and I can always savor and enjoy the past! What's more, the front is so unpredictable: maybe the train will pass through a barren desert, drill into a deep cave! Or encounter unexpected obstacles and derail! Maybe the plane will encounter a violent gale and capsize, encounter a misty fog and lose its direction, or suddenly run out of engine oil and fall!

However, in fact, the cruel and ruthless "time", it stubbornly insisted on me moving forward, it would not let me retreat, it grabbed me so tightly! I repeatedly looked back reluctantly, but the further I looked, the further it became! So I closed my eyelids and thought carefully and silently – batches of scattered memories, vaguely and in groups, filled my heart. Is it always possible to get only by greedily reminiscing about the past? "Impossible"! It answered me like this. It also told me to stare at the front, because there is still a "future" ahead!

Staring at the "future" is too difficult for me! My weak vision cannot penetrate this current vague "future"! I only see a vast expanse of white! Abyss, jagged rocks, vines, stubborn stones, and unpredictable and terrible attacks, can I cross them? Can I resist them?············

If what I have walked in the past is a flat and broad road, then what I will walk in the future will be a rugged and narrow path. I accidentally walked so many roads, and thinking about it was ignorant and absurd, and although I am still safe and sound today, I already feel very disheartened! What's more, once I discovered the unpredictability and danger of the future, how could I not be frightened?

Ah! The future! The future is terrifying! Even if someone says the future is bright!

Work No. 3 from the Songjiang Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition: Mr. Song Junyang's Calligraphy

Work No. 4: Mr. Huang Zongxiang's Recent Work

Melancholy Lilac

— Simon

Facing the back window of the house of worship, there is a small private garden in the neighborhood. In the early morning, the crisp chimes of the church are rippling in the misty air, and each flower in the garden is bathed in crystal-cracked heavy dew. I stand in front of the window, listening to the gentle music-like chimes, and looking at each flower swaying with a sleepy and charming attitude, swaying lightly in the slight morning breeze.

It is a poetic, illusory, and heart-pleasing poetic morning!

For this garden, which is so gorgeously decorated by nature, I can use more time and more

Page 19

intoxicated mood to appreciate it. Especially unforgettable is the scene every evening, when the faint afterglow of the setting sun faintly strokes the towering spire of the church, stroking the quiet and beautiful little garden, so lingering as if reluctant to leave. The meaning at this time is even a bit close to the mysterious.

Every day, whether in the evening or in the early morning, I make sure to come to this window and linger for a while, and I have become accustomed to it for many days. Because standing there and looking at such scenery, the depressed mind will often relax immediately. But I often feel a disappointment. This garden, which is planted with all kinds of flowers, is uniquely lacking the light and graceful shadow of lilac. I wonder why the owner of the garden simply doesn't want lilac. Although I admire this garden for having all kinds of colorful flowers, I don't like peach blossoms that are too gorgeous, and roses that are too gorgeous. The strong fragrance will instead make people feel breathless. What I like is the purple lilac, which is neither too gorgeous nor too faint, like a slender, elegant, and silent girl.

However, I have never seen the lilac that I want.

One early morning, as usual, I walked to the back window again, looking with more meticulous scrutiny than usual, hoping to find it. After looking at it several times, when my sight reached the place where the grape trellis used to be, the shadow of the West cluster of lilac suddenly reflected into my eyes. If the grape trellis were not removed, the lilac would bloom and wither silently for the rest of its life.

Lilac can now "smile in the sun, right? But no, because in the long days of the past, it was buried under the grape trellis, without the nourishment of the sun and the cultivation of dew. It has made it as unsmiling as a patient, with its face shrouded in the dark clouds of deep sorrow. Infinite melancholy surrounds the small branches and leaves, and the small soul? The color of youth is withering unnamed in the bleak destiny. The miserable body droops weakly to the ground.

I couldn't help but become inexplicably melancholy for the melancholy of lilac.

I couldn't help but curse that grape trellis on behalf of lilac. It made it spend dark days without sunshine or happiness in silence, and it also made it silently approach withering without ever having a brilliant youth. All the unfortunate encounters were all given by the abominable grape trellis. Without the grape trellis, it would have appeared in this garden more happily and vividly than its other companions.

Maybe it would have been appreciated by the owner. But everything was destroyed by the grape trellis.

And I can only stare at your gloomy and haggard shadow from afar on this window, sighing for your misfortune.

No one would have imagined that on another early morning, just as I was walking to the window, suddenly two young girls were walking on the pebble road, each picking a handful of fresh flowers, holding them in their hands, some red and some purple. When I moved my eyes to the position of lilac, the purple lilac had lost its melancholy shadow. Only a pile of loose soil remained. Only then did I realize that it had been placed in the hand of that girl. It looked a little bleak for a moment.

Being taken away by a young girl may get better treatment once, carefully supplying it to a gilded clean bottle, but tomorrow it will inevitably wither very quickly. Tomorrow there will be fresh ones to replace the withered ones of yesterday. But the melancholy lilac, your melancholy shadow, will never fade in my memory. ······

Storytelling Venue

— Jue

Since coming to Beiping, although not many days have passed, I have been to the storytelling venue several times. The reason is that the place is so quiet and cold. When night falls, sitting alone in a room like an ancient temple, listening quietly to the sound of the clapper vibrating in the night sky, and the cries of hawkers, ······ it becomes even more desolate and silent, which makes people unbearable. Therefore, listening to storytelling has gradually become my only job when I am bored.

The storytelling venue in this place is very old-fashioned.

Usually, in a hall of about one or two zhang square, a dirt platform more than a foot high and five or six feet wide is built against one side of the wall, with a table, two chairs, and a tripod drum stand placed on it. Next to the platform, there is a seat for boiling water and selling tea. Under the platform, six or seven tea tables and more than a dozen long benches are tightly arranged. This is the complete equipment of a complete storytelling venue. If you accidentally walk past the door before the show starts and peek inside, you may not believe that such a place is an entertainment venue. Not to mention other things, just take a tour of various "modern" entertainment venues and then come back here to take a look, and you will feel as if time has been pulled back one or two hundred years.

During the day, this place is very deserted. Usually, there is only an old man with fluent speech sitting listlessly on the stage, telling stories of "The Romance of the Three Kingdoms", "Water Margin", ······ and other "big books". The audience is only a few job leavers and children. But when night falls, it becomes much more lively. At this time, the storytellers who take the stage are mostly young women. At the same time, when telling stories, there are also people playing the sanxian and erhu to accompany them. The books they tell are either about talented scholars and beautiful women, or about Wu Song fighting the tiger on Jingyang Ridge, Zhao Zilong rescuing the lord on Changban Slope, ······ and other heroic stories. Among the audience, there are old shop clerks, small vendors and coolies, and widowed old ladies, ······ Every time a story is sung, everyone holds their breath and stares intently, watching as if they are mesmerized. After a story is sung, someone walks down from the stage, holding a small bamboo basket in their hand, walks past one table after another, and asks the audience for money. The guests can take out one or two copper coins and throw them into the basket at will. No one will force them. However, the person who collects the money is very clever. Every time they collect money, if it does not meet the amount they expected, they will always say a lot of difficult words to the guests as if by magic, and then come again once, twice, ······ They will only stop asking when they can't ask any more. Or, if a cunning guest throws three or two copper coins at the pile of money in the basket with force, making a "sha ······" sound, then he will raise his voice and report to the person in charge on the stage: ×× table gave × hanging of money, making the other guests embarrassed to be too stingy with their own wallets. Therefore, if you are a regular customer and familiar with these tricks they play, you can spend one or two hours here with a dozen or so copper coins in your pocket; but, if you are a new customer, you have to spend at least one or two jiao a night.

A place of entertainment like this will naturally not attract the attention of the noble; but, its impact on the masses is not to be underestimated. I think that a group of artists who often shout "for the masses" in their mouths, if they are willing to take the trouble to come here and take a look, they will not cause trouble for themselves, right?

Beggar

— Translated by Yi from Tugenev

I was walking down the street... An elderly beggar stopped me.

His red, swollen eyes were filled with tears, his lips were turning blue, his clothes were ragged, his wounds were filthy... Ah, how terrible, poverty had eroded this unfortunate life!

He reached out a red, swollen, and filthy hand to me... He groaned, pleading for help.

So I searched my own pockets... No wallet, no watch, not even a handkerchief... I had nothing on me.

But the beggar waited... his outstretched hand trembling.

I was moved, confused, and firmly grasped his filthy, trembling hand, saying: "Friend, do not be disappointed; I have nothing at all, friend."

The beggar's red, swollen eyes stared at me, a smile now on his blue lips... He, too, gripped my hand tightly with his cold fingers.

"What, friend," he said softly, "even so, I must thank you, this is also a kind of charity, friend."

I understood, I too, had received charity from him.

Movie Stage Coffee Shop

— Jiang Manlang

The young man who teaches Japanese is from Tokyo, without father, mother, wife, or family. His studies were supported by others. (In Japan, there are many such examples; a capitalist or politician will support at least a few poor students.) Although he has now graduated from a specialized school, he has not yet found a job, but he still wants to have fun, spending whatever money he has on food and entertainment. This is probably the spirit of urban youth. The person who introduced him to me first told us about this habit, and if we want to learn a few more words, we can only exploit this weakness.

The first time, I went with him to Ginza to see a movie. The first movie was about a poor man and a child struggling to survive in the city, somewhat imitating Charlie Chaplin's bittersweet comedies (i.e., “Water Suicide”). Another was about a young man's suffering from love and life, and his suicide with a geisha. Japanese national character: courage, righteousness, enthusiasm, and narrow-mindedness. A spirit of going forward without looking back, even to death, can be seen here.

Regarding Tokyo's dance performances, we watched the Shochiku Girls' Opera's "Ode to the Night," "Rose," and "Paris" at the Shinjuku First Theater. The dazzling lights and luxurious extravagance were overwhelming. The number of dancers alone was one or two hundred. The sheer number, the gorgeous colors, and the sensual abundance were only meant to stimulate the audience; there was nothing else to appreciate. What was commendable was the speed of the stage setup, which was probably due to mechanization, because the stage could rotate.

The most popular dance star here is Tatsuko Mizunoe. Japanese women's magazines frequently feature her photos, life stories, and biographies. Women, in particular, are fond of her because she plays male roles best. This is similar to how Chinese people like Mei Lanfang's male impersonation of female roles. This kind of "sexual disguise" probably only exists in the most Confucian societies.

There are two types of coffee shops: one that purely sells coffee and food, and another that sells smiles. Because one of the gentlemen who came to Tokyo with me was a hedonist, he went to a "smile-selling" coffee shop in Osaka, sat for a while, and joked around, which cost six or seven yuan. I went with him again in Tokyo. The Japanese women's softness and the prostitutes' vulgarity were fully on display. As an objective observer, I felt that this was not heaven, but certainly not paradise. It could only be described as the crystallization of hell.

However, many students studying in Tokyo become addicted to this path, which is lamentable.

Chinese Studies

Ms. Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Song of Changgan (Part 1) by Li Bai

My hair just covered my forehead, playing with flowers in front of the gate. My love came riding a bamboo horse,

circling the bed, playing with green plums. Living together in Changgan Village, as children, we were without suspicion.

At fourteen, I became your wife, my face shy, never opening up. I lowered my head to the dark wall,

no matter how many times you called, I would not respond. At fifteen, I began to smile, willing to be as dust and ashes with you.

Always cherishing the embrace-the-pillar promise, how could I ascend the Looking-for-Husband Terrace. At sixteen, you went on a long journey,

to the treacherous Qutang Gorge. The fifth month is not to be touched, the sound of monkeys wailing in the sky.

Footprints linger before the gate, one by one covered in green moss. The moss is too deep to sweep away,

falling leaves, early autumn wind. In the eighth month, butterflies come, flying in pairs in the west garden grass.

Moved by this, my heart is saddened, sitting and worrying about my fading beauty! Sooner or later I will go down to Sanba,

and send a letter home in advance. To greet you, I will not say it is far, I will go straight to Changfengsha.

Shanghai News Local Supplement Auto Weekly

Prelude to the American Automobile Industry in 1935

— Ling Yun

丨Refilling Old Capacity Will Increase Threefold丨

The raw materials for automobile manufacturing include steel, copper, lead, zinc, and other metals. Because the automobile manufacturing industry is developed in the United States, the annual consumption of the above-mentioned metals is very considerable. Taking tin as an example, the annual amount used for automobile manufacturing accounts for 25% of the normal annual tin production in the United States. Therefore, it is generally recognized that if the American automobile industry can revive, other industries will also benefit from it. According to the current situation, the automobile industry is indeed undergoing revival. In the near future, we will see significant progress. Both production and sales will increase significantly. Taking the facts as an example, it can prove that this is correct. Because the automobile production volume in 1934 has already told us that there is a significant improvement. As for 1935, needless to say, it will continue to move forward and head towards a bright road.

Based on the current situation and past experience, the driving forces that can influence the increase in automobile sales are roughly the following three points. (1) The reason for refilling old cars. People who have bought cars cannot be expected to never add new cars in their lifetime. Therefore, after a considerable period of a few years, a batch of new cars will be used to replace the old ones. (2) Due to the prosperity and improvement of various industries. We all know that the automobile industry and other industries have a mutually linked circular relationship. If all industries decline and the social economy is exhausted, the sales of automobiles will naturally be greatly affected. Conversely, if society shows prosperity and everyone has purchasing power, automobiles will undoubtedly sell well. It is also no problem for the factory to increase its revenue. (3) The reason for the federal government's allocation of funds to farmers. Farmers need cars no less than urban residents. They use cars and tractors to cultivate and improve their production efficiency. However, farmers naturally have no money to buy cars because of the decline of rural areas. For the sake of relief, the federal government allocated funds to them, so the sales of automobiles will naturally also increase. Whether other industries besides the automobile industry can continue to recover and improve without decline in 1935 is still unknown. Therefore, the second point mentioned above is not very reliable in terms of its impact on increasing automobile sales. We will leave it aside for now and only talk about the first and third points, which are inevitable. There is no doubt that they will affect the increase in automobile sales. These two reasons were very effective in 1934. As Claim's automobile report stated, the American automobile production in the autumn of 1934 totaled 696,851 units. This number is the largest production volume in the third quarter of each year since 1930. Because of various reasons, automobile sales in winter are relatively sluggish. It is also expected that the autumn season is better than the fourth quarter of each year. This quantity increased by 3.6% compared to the same period in 1933.

In the first nine months of 1934, the sales of automobiles in the United States totaled 2,493,260 units, an increase of 18.2% compared to the same period in 1930. The production volume in the winter of 1934 was of course lower, as mentioned above. However, according to the estimates of powerful people, the total production volume for the year was about 2,778,000 units. This total increased by 12.2% compared to 1933, and decreased by 20.5% compared to 1930. Because the total production volume in that year was 3,510,178 units. It is not easy to say how much the recovery of various industries and the federal government's allocation of funds have increased automobile sales. However, the quantity of regular refilling of old cars can be calculated. There is continuous progress in the refilling of old cars. If old cars are not refilled for several years, the quantity will accumulate. Therefore, from this point alone, we can be optimistic. The average number of new private passenger cars and commercial vehicles sold in the United States in the past four years was 2,068,794 units. The average number in the previous five years was 3,546,130 units. What we should pay attention to here is that this five-year period includes the peak sales years of 1928 and 1929. However, in fact, the cars sold in those two years now need to be refilled. Unless the car owner is unable to add or replace new cars in this recessionary period due to poor economic conditions. There is also one more thing. In the past three years, there have been few car owners who have purchased new cars. The situation is the same for those who have purchased multiple cars. Therefore, the matter of refilling old cars is relatively certain.

According to the calculation of the American National Automobile Association, the lifespan of a car is currently about seven years and eight months. In 1929, it was six years and nine months. Even if we say that the average lifespan of a car is eight years, then the number of old cars that will expire in 1935 should be 7,000,000 units. This number will increase threefold compared to the estimated total production volume in 1934. Speaking of the existing number of automobiles in the United States, it has decreased by 2,700,000 units since 1930. Under the current circumstances, I am afraid that many car owners will still not be able to purchase new cars. However, even if we subtract the number of unregistered cars, the number of old cars to be refilled will still be more than twice that of 1933. If it is unreliable to say that the American automobile industry in 1935 will cope with all needs with 7,000,000 units, then its huge quantity of old cars to be refilled will of course be recognized by more people.

The New Lineup of Standard Motors

— Shadow Viewer

Firm Position, Excellent Products

(1) The Pressure of the Environment Approximately eighteen months ago, the directors of Standard Motors sat together to consider the 1934 business plan. They acknowledged that the revival of the automobile industry was imminent. The recessionary atmosphere of 1931 would become a thing of the past, and the sales of automobiles would increase in the transition from 1933 to 1934. Many car owners should have replaced their cars from 1932 or 1933, but for economic reasons, they did not purchase new vehicles. Therefore, after the situation improved, private car orders would suddenly become active. On the other hand, automobile manufacturing had undergone many improvements and new trends. Small engines could increase horsepower. In addition to increasing the speed of cars, gearbox shifting was also more convenient. Research and experimentation progressed simultaneously, making engine operation silent and smooth, without any inconvenience. Other improvements included the ability to handle uneven roads, reduced weight, elimination of wind resistance, and even touring cars possessed these advantages. The improvement of materials and the reduction of labor wages, both directly and indirectly, would increase vehicle sales.

(2) A Grand Plan In this situation, the board of directors of Standard Motors reached a resolution. Their various vehicles with "Nine Horsepower," small "Nine Horsepower," "Twelve Horsepower," "Sixteen Horsepower," and "Twenty Horsepower" engines were all excellent cars. They had considerable sales in the recession years. However, despite these vehicles being finely manufactured and sturdy, in the trend of automobile progress, they undoubtedly needed to be improved. Otherwise, there would be the possibility of failure and elimination. Therefore, they worked tirelessly. In the automotive market, the damage inflicted by the recession had not yet recovered. The factory had to work hard, and they purchased many new instruments and raw materials, and built new factories. Standard Motors was determined to work tirelessly under the will to revive the automobile industry.

(3) Manufacturing New Cars In September 1933, Standard Motors announced that the above-mentioned five types of completely renovated new cars had been fully completed. The engine styles and designs, car bodies, chassis, and transmissions were completely revamped. The accessories were complete. The launch of the new cars was earlier than expected. The success achieved after the launch of the 1934 Standard new cars exceeded the initial expectations of the board of directors when they decided on the new strategy. In terms of business, countless orders were soon received. Thereafter, sales continued to improve. In the social aspect, many people purchased a Standard new car. Until June 30, 1934, Standard had manufactured and sold more than 20,000 vehicles in the market.

(4) Owner's Testimonials From past experience, we know that every car factory, when manufacturing new cars, is cautious and careful, and conducts thorough inspections, hoping that the new cars will be free of defects after they are manufactured. However, occasional minor flaws are unavoidable. Therefore, once a new car is launched, some minor shortcomings will be discovered before twenty vehicles are produced. However, car owners, who are generally accustomed to criticizing, use these shortcomings as information to point out flaws. So, in fact, a perfect new car rarely receives good reviews at the beginning. Inconvenient movement of the sunroof, excessive angle when moving the gear lever, and poorly placed door buttons are all minor problems, but harsh critics insist on using them as good material for nitpicking. However, the Standard new cars, after their launch, did not have these minor problems at all. They were truly the most perfect new cars. The action, driving, luster, silence, comfort, and appearance were absolutely flawless. Therefore, after the new cars were launched, they received unexpectedly good reviews from general critics. Standard Motors' slogan "Manufacturing cars that society needs" is appropriate. Society needs such a car. This is the reason why the sales of Standard cars will increase day by day.

(5) Expansion of Scope These new cars had considerable success in 1934. The 1935 new cars retained their various advantages. There were many improvements in manufacturing. Basically, after a year of testing, people were very satisfied and there were no changes, because society had already proven them to be excellent. However, in addition to the above types, two new cars were added. One was a specially modified "Nine Straight" new car with a slightly longer wheelbase and a four-door sedan body. The other was the "Ten/Twelve Special Speed" new car. This new car completely occupied a new field. In terms of appearance, it was completely the same as the 1935 "Ten Horsepower" Standard new car, but inside, it possessed a special performance that would satisfy every traveler. The top speed could reach an average of 70 miles per hour. In terms of acceleration (which was the result of testing in various climates and on different roads), it could accelerate from a complete stop to 50 miles per hour in 16 seconds. What was especially mysterious was a specially made engine with a capacity of 1608 cubic centimeters, with dual carburetors and an aluminum cylinder head. Therefore, if we add up the old cars that Standard's 1935 new cars have successfully improved over the past year, and the completely new cars manufactured this year, there are the following types: (1) "Nine Horsepower" new car (two-door and four-door). (2) "Ten Horsepower" new car. (3) "Twelve Horsepower" new car. (4) "Ten/Twelve" Special Speed new car. (5) "Sixteen Horsepower" new car. (6) "Twenty Horsepower" new car.

The above are all British standard new cars, representing the products. In the coming year, the sales of the 1935 Standard new cars will undoubtedly exceed the record of 1934.

Austin Sales Increase Sharply

Employing 19,000 Workers

According to news from the Austin factory, the number of workers currently employed by the factory has broken all previous records, with the current number being 19,000, an increase of more than 1,500 compared to a month ago. As for the reason for the increase in the number of people, it is naturally due to busy work. The reason for the busy work is due to the sharp increase in the sales of the globally renowned Austin cars. This is self-evident. According to the factory's products, the 7-horsepower and 10-horsepower four-cylinder new cars are in the greatest demand. Since the factory increased the number of people, the production volume has increased, which is sufficient to adapt to the growing demand. As of now, the sales of the small Austin new cars have exceeded 20% compared to the same period last year. The sales last year were already amazing, but now they have surpassed them, which is especially commendable.

Dodge Factory Manufactures a Large Number of New Cars

Orders Valued at 40 Million Yuan

According to a telegram from Detroit, USA, on January 28, orders for cars and trucks worth 40 million yuan have been delivered by Dodge dealers in various states to the special commissioners stationed in 25 cities by the factory. According to Mr. Vanderkie, General Manager of the Dodge Company's marketing department, the 1935 Dodge new cars have been exhibited in various cities.

Ford's Success in the Finnish Rally

From October 20 to 21 last year, in the first annual rally of the Finnish Automobile Club, Ford cars won twelve of the fifteen top prizes, and nine of them reached the finish line without any damage.

This trial was based on the Monte Carlo Rally. It started from various places in Finland and had to travel 850 miles to Helsinki. The journey was extremely difficult due to heavy rain and snow.

Each stage had a strict timetable. Competitors would be penalized for every minute of loss or any damage to the exterior of their cars.

Among the 25 competitors in the Mita class cars with a cubic capacity of over 1500 C.C., twelve reached the finish line without any loss of points. No less than nine of them were driving Ford cars, mostly V8 models.

Most of the special prizes were also won by Ford drivers. One of them was the Hua Da Memorial Prize, which was won by Ms. Jialindaer because she drove her V8 with exceptional skill.

Ford's success in this competition has attracted widespread attention from the Finnish automobile industry and the general public.
