Supplement to the Shanghai Shen Bao 本埠增刊, Movie Special Edition

A Burned Love Letter in the Home of Pat O'Brien

— Ti Yun

Pat O'Brien's family is one of the happiest families in Hollywood, but the success of this family and the happiness of the two of them are due to the recovery of a lost letter. Otherwise, their future would be unpredictable. Perhaps they would have failed, and even their names would not be heard.

The lost letter was an airmail letter. The plane crashed and the letter was lost. But that letter was the lifeline of both of them. Half a year later, the letter was rediscovered, and their new life began again. What a dangerous thing it was!

Almost six years ago, Pat O'Brien and Eloise Taylor were both acting in a theater troupe in Chicago. Their romance was known to everyone. They were madly in love and planned to get married on the first day of the break after a season and go on their honeymoon. That night was the last night of the season, and for Eloise, it was the last time in her life to be on stage. She loved Pat so much that she was willing to sacrifice her own future to be Pat's good wife. She believed that Pat's future would be successful. He would soon be on stage on Broadway in New York. They both had unlimited hope.

But that very night, they quarreled. It was a very fierce quarrel because it was the first quarrel. The reason was a very minor thing, and even they themselves could not say what it was. But Pat's strong Irish temper was uncontrollable. He said things that he would not normally say. Eloise also had her own temper. They soon began to scold each other, saying things that did not make sense. But they agreed on one point... that their romance was a foolish move and that their marriage would be a lifelong mistake, so it was better to break up now! They both said that they would never see each other again!

Their quarrel took place backstage in the theater. After the quarrel, Pat immediately returned to his residence, packed his bags, and took the train to New York that night. But after the train left, Pat's temper slowly subsided. When he arrived in New York, he was very remorseful and scolded himself for doing such a stupid thing. He wanted to take the original train back to Chicago immediately, but he remembered that Eloise had said that she would never see him again, and perhaps that was her true feeling. So he thought it was better to write a letter to apologize first.

He arrived at the inn and immediately wrote a letter to Eloise. He used ten large sheets of paper to finish writing the elegy in his heart, all kinds of apologies, asking her to forgive him. Finally, he also said that if she did not reply immediately, he would think that she really did not want to see him, but he would not blame her, because she knew that he was not worthy of loving her.

He sent the letter by airmail. Since then, he has been waiting for a reply all the time. When the phone rang or someone knocked on the door, he would jump up, but he waited day after day, but there was no news. In his disappointment, the play he was performing also failed. He was almost impoverished and bored to the point of suicide. In this way, he endured day after day for six months. Suddenly one day, he received a letter from the government, and when he opened it, it was the long letter he had sent to Eloise six months ago. The letter had been burned beyond recognition. Fortunately, the address of the sender was still vaguely visible, so he tried to return it. It turned out that the plane had crashed, and his letter had never been delivered.

Pat received the returned letter and immediately rushed to the telegraph office to send a long telegram to Eloise's home, almost as long as that letter. He then returned to the inn and waited anxiously again. But this time he did not have to wait long. He received a telegram from Eloise saying that she had already forgiven him and that she had been regretting it every day since they parted. Pat received the telegram and did not reply to her again. He didn't have time to pack his bags, just grabbed a toothbrush, and immediately rushed to where Eloise lived. As soon as he arrived there, they got married that day.

That was more than five years ago. Since they got married, Pat O'Brien has been sailing smoothly, without any setbacks. He returned to the stage in New York and won great acclaim in the theater world. Hollywood heard his name and hired him to make movies. He still attributes his success to the help of his wife. As for the burned letter, they framed it and hung it in the study. Every time they were about to quarrel, they just looked at the frame and laughed it off.

A Hollywood Insider Says

— Qi Guan

A Hollywood insider said: "If you take the copies of the 57 films directed by Cecil B. DeMille and connect them together, they can circle the earth east and west, and then circle the earth north and south."

"If a person gets permission from the owners of the New York and Los Angeles theaters to take a day's box office revenue as their own, they can immediately become a millionaire."

"If the MGM studio needs to completely replace new equipment due to an incident, all the goods in the largest department store in New York City would not be one-third of what is moved out of the MGM studio. In other words, the equipment moved out of the MGM studio can open three or more of the largest department stores in New York."

"If you take the world's largest screen in the New York Paramount Company and move it to the ground, three hundred people can stand on it very sparsely."

"There are a total of 14,900 cinemas in Europe, but that is still 7,100 fewer than the number of cinemas in the United States alone."

"If a person can gather all the income from American cinemas in one month, no rich man in the world can compete with him. This number is really difficult to calculate."

"The world's largest open-air cinema is at the foot of Beverly Hills in Hollywood. If it is used as an airport in winter when it is not in use, it can accommodate as many as 50 German Junkers aircraft."

"If Paramount Pictures Corporation were to clear out its interior and auction off all the wheels, it could open a large automobile company. In addition to those used by stars and directors and for private use, there are 3,200 vehicles."

"If all the planes in the various film companies in Hollywood were to take off and fly in the sky over Honolulu, many people would definitely think that military action had started in Honolulu the next day."

"The Eternal Family," currently in production

Zhong Shigen's great work "The Eternal Family," after "Life," is being co-directed by Luo Mingyou and Fei Mu, and production has already begun. The grandeur of this drama can be described as unprecedented in the Chinese silver screen for several years. The richness and moving nature of the content is undoubtedly due to the fact that you cannot find anything empty and boring in Zhong's script. As for the cast, this time it can almost be called a collaboration of all the stars. Lin Chuchu, Chen Yanyan, Li Zhuozhuo; Zhang Yi, Zheng Junli, Li Keng, Shang Guanwu, Mei Lin... are all showing their talents here. This drama writes the story of three couples in three eras, Shang Guanwu and Lin Chuchu, Zhang Yi and Li Zhuozhuo, Zheng Junli and Mei Lin. Chen Yanyan plays the daughter of Chuchu Guanwu, and Li Keng is the young Zheng Junli. Now, the scenes being filmed are all the important scenes of Lin Chuchu and Chen Yanyan, because the scenes being filmed are very emotional, so they can all be truly emotional, especially the tragic parts are very fruitful.

A scene from "A Chorus of Women"—Nanjing Screening, starring Snow Murray Howard, the master of comedy

Wang Renmei Cries Bitterly

Everyone knows that Wang Renmei is a jumping, forever carefree wildcat. But when Xu Xingzhi told her that in this scene she had to hug Mu Zhi and cry bitterly, the more sad the better, and that this was a climax in "Sons and Daughters in a Time of Storm" and was very important to the whole drama, she immediately stopped smiling and became dazed.

Yes, crying bitterly and shedding tears is really too difficult for a carefree wildcat. So she sat blankly on the sofa until Xingzhi told her to start shooting, and she still stood up blankly, walked to Yuan Muzhi, hugged him, and remained silent.

After Xingzhi's "Camera rolling!" was shouted, Renmei began to sob and cry, and she cried so sadly that everyone on the set thought she was pretending to cry, but everyone was surprised at how she could cry so realistically.

But after Muzhi raised his face, he saw that she was already in tears, and she was crying more and more sadly. This made Xingzhi anxious, and he quickly shouted "Cut!" Perhaps she couldn't control the bursting emotions! Renmei sat on the sofa and still cried non-stop. Xingzhi persuaded her for a while before she stopped crying.

Afterwards, Situ Huimin ran out of the sound room and said to Xingzhi that Renmei's crying in this scene was so moving when it was broadcast on the radio.

Special Issue of "The Red Goat Biography"

— Run

"The Legend of the Red Goat Hero" is the first historical sound film produced in our country. Since Xinhua Film Company has made this great contribution, it is also carrying out a special issue, edited by novelists Wang Zhongxian and Zheng Yimei. The content includes dozens of copper and zinc版 photographs, and the texts are all written by famous writers, such as Yan Duhe's "Consciousness on the Silver Screen," Zhang Henshui's "The Taiping Heavenly Kingdom's Politics Deserves Praise," Fan Yanqiao's "Exposing the Revolutionary Consciousness for the Taiping Army," Shuliu Mountain Room's "Recording Zeng's Army's Attack on Ning," Jiang Yinqiu's "The Mission of the Red Goat Hero," Zhao Huanting's "Anecdotes about the Red Goat Hero," and so on, totaling tens of thousands of words. The film will be released in theaters on the Lunar New Year's Day, and will be sold in theaters.

Regular Performances by the Stage Association

The Shanghai Stage Association is an organization formed by well-known figures in the Shanghai film and theater circles. It has recently begun preparations for its first public performance. It is reported that the repertoire for the public performance has been determined to be two types: "Under the Mercury Lamp" (one act) and "The Song of Rejuvenation" (three acts). They are now rehearsing day and night, and have chosen to perform for several days starting from the 30th of this month at the Jincheng Grand Theater on Beijing Road. The association is full of talented people, and it will definitely be able to add a special color to the theater world in the New Year.

Film Novel

The Red Sheep Gallants, Part 9

— Zhao Chu

Zeng and Shi arrived at the Gui Ping county yamen and waited in the reception hall. Zeng said, "If he accepts our silver, the matter will be settled." Just as he was speaking, an elderly man resembling a yamen secretary, wearing glasses, came out from within. Smiling at them, he cupped his hands and said, "Congratulations, congratulations! The matter has finally been settled." The elderly man urgently continued, "The matter almost stalled. He was unwilling to accept it. I said that Mr. Wei's crime was only a fabrication by Vice General Li, lacking any real evidence, and it would be best to do a favor." Only then was the matter settled. Zeng Yuheng hurriedly cupped his hands in greeting and said, "Fortunately, we relied on Master Wang's great efforts. We are truly grateful." As he spoke, he took out a small package from his pocket and handed it to the old man, saying, "This small token expresses our gratitude." The old man repeatedly declined, but in the end, he accepted it, saying, "Mr. Wei will surely be safely home tomorrow. The two of you can rest assured." Thereupon, Zeng and Shi expressed their gratitude and took their leave.

The next day, Li Dianyuan was in the process of reviewing official documents when the clerk hurriedly rushed in and said to Li, "Wei Changhui was released by the magistrate early this morning. I heard that someone went to the county to pull strings yesterday and obtained a lot of illicit money." Upon hearing this, Vice General Li stood up in anger and scolded, "He clearly wants to deceive me! He is being too insolent! We are both officials of the imperial court; how can I let him get away with this?!" As he spoke, he smashed the teacup in his hand on the ground. Vice General Li paced back and forth in the room and then turned back to the clerk and said, "Quickly prepare thirty mounted escorts! I will personally bring Wei Changhui back!" The clerk agreed and hurriedly turned to leave.

On the road out of the city, Wei Changhui looked very dejected. He was being carried in a soft chair by two men. An old family servant supported him from the side, saying, "Young Master, this is truly an unprovoked disaster. You have suffered this terrible punishment for no reason." Changhui sighed and said, "In this world, is there any right or wrong, black or white?" As he spoke, he continued forward. Unexpectedly, Vice General Li led more than twenty riders, galloping towards them. Wei Changhui's sedan chair arrived in front of the Wei family ancestral hall and stopped for a temporary rest. Vice General Li's men arrived soon after. Upon seeing Wei, Li immediately dismounted, walked up to Wei, and grabbed him. The old family servant stepped forward to protect him but was pushed to the ground. Vice General Li asked very fiercely, "How did you escape?" Wei replied, "The county released me because I am innocent. How can you say I escaped?" Li, in extreme anger, cursed, "How dare you not go through my interrogation?!" As he spoke, he snatched the whip from an attendant's hand and lashed it fiercely at Wei's face. Then he kicked Wei, knocking him to the ground. Li then shouted to the soldiers, "Quickly tie him up! I will personally interrogate him!" Thereupon, several soldiers stepped forward and tied him to a tree. Vice General Li, holding the whip in one hand, tore off Wei's clothes, saying, "Why don't you get the county to protect you?" As he spoke, he lashed down with the whip again. The old family servant, hearing the sound of the beating, stealthily hid behind people and ran away. The villagers all around gathered to watch. Some of the elders said, "Why is it Young Master Wei being beaten?" Wei Changhui endured the beating, almost fainting, moaning incessantly. Vice General Li, in extreme ferocity, beat him while saying, "Let's see what you have to say for yourself!"

Shi Dakai, Zeng Yuheng, and Yang Xiuqing were sitting in the Wei family's main hall, talking with Wei's father. Zeng Yuheng said, "Brother Wei should be back soon." Just as he said this, the old family servant, his head bleeding, walked in in a disheveled state, and said in a flustered manner, "We were halfway back when that Vice General Li chased after us again, tied the young master to a tree and is whipping him. He is almost beating him to death now." As he spoke, he cried out in sorrow and indignation. (To be continued)
